# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": DSInt(),
    "height": DSInt()
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "item_name": float,
    "box_number": DSInt(),
    "x_position": DSInt(),
    "y_position": DSInt()
})

Box = DSRecord({
    "width": DSInt(),
    "height": DSInt()
})

# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT: int = 6
BOX_WIDTH: int = 10
N_ITEMS: int = 6
ITEM1_WIDTH: int = 4
ITEM1_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM2_WIDTH: int = 3
ITEM2_HEIGHT: int = 2
ITEM3_WIDTH: int = 5
ITEM3_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM4_WIDTH: int = 2
ITEM4_HEIGHT: int = 4
ITEM5_WIDTH: int = 3
ITEM5_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM6_WIDTH: int = 5
ITEM6_HEIGHT: int = 2
nr_used_boxes : DSInt(1, N_ITEMS)
item_box_assignment : DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment)
x_y_positions : DSList(N_ITEMS, DSRecord({'x': DSInt(), 'y': DSInt() }))

# --- Decision Variables ---
chosen_items : DSList(N_ITEMS, DSBool())

# --- Constraints ---
def fit_item_in_box(item: Item, box: Box, x_position: DSInt(), y_position: DSInt()):
    assert x_position >= 0
    assert x_position + item.width <= box.width
    assert y_position >= 0
    assert y_position + item.height <= box.height

def assign_items_to_boxes(items: DSList(N_ITEMS, Item), box_assignment: DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment), boxes: DSList(N_ITEMS, Box)):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        box_assignment_item: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[i]
        box: Box = boxes[box_assignment_item.box_number]
        fit_item_in_box(item, box, box_assignment_item.x_position, box_assignment_item.y_position)

# --- Objective ---
def calculate_objective(items: DSList(N_ITEMS, Item), box_assignment: DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment)):
    objective: int = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        box_assignment_item: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[i]
        objective = objective + item.width * item.height
    return objective

# --- Initialization ---
items : DSList(N_ITEMS, Item) = [
    {"width": ITEM1_WIDTH, "height": ITEM1_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM2_WIDTH, "height": ITEM2_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM3_WIDTH, "height": ITEM3_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM4_WIDTH, "height": ITEM4_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM5_WIDTH, "height": ITEM5_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM6_WIDTH, "height": ITEM6_HEIGHT}
]

        box: Box = boxes[box_assignment_item.box_number]
        fit_item_in_box(item, box, box_assignment_item.x_position, box_assignment_item.y_position)

def non_overlapping_items(items: DSList(N_ITEMS, Item), box_assignment: DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment)):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            box_assignment_item_i: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[i]
            box_assignment_item_j: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[j]
            item_i: Item = items[i]
            item_j: Item = items[j]
            if box_assignment_item_i.box_number == box_assignment_item_j.box_number:
                assert box_assignment_item_i.x_position + item_i.width <= box_assignment_item_j.x_position or \
                       box_assignment_item_j.x_position + item_j.width <= box_assignment_item_i.x_position or \
                       box_assignment_item_i.y_position + item_i.height <= box_assignment_item_j.y_position or \
                       box_assignment_item_j.y_position + item_j.height <= box_assignment_item_i.y_position

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": DSInt(),
    "height": DSInt()
})

BoxAssignment = DSRecord({
    "item_name": float,
    "box_number": DSInt(),
    "x_position": DSInt(),
    "y_position": DSInt()
})

Box = DSRecord({
    "width": DSInt(),
    "height": DSInt()
})



# --- Constants ---
BOX_HEIGHT: int = 6
BOX_WIDTH: int = 10
N_ITEMS: int = 6
ITEM1_WIDTH: int = 4
ITEM1_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM2_WIDTH: int = 3
ITEM2_HEIGHT: int = 2
ITEM3_WIDTH: int = 5
ITEM3_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM4_WIDTH: int = 2
ITEM4_HEIGHT: int = 4
ITEM5_WIDTH: int = 3
ITEM5_HEIGHT: int = 3
ITEM6_WIDTH: int = 5
ITEM6_HEIGHT: int = 2
nr_used_boxes : DSInt(1, N_ITEMS)
item_box_assignment : DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment)
x_y_positions : DSList(N_ITEMS, DSRecord({'x': DSInt(), 'y': DSInt() }))


# -- Constraints --

# --- Decision Variables ---
chosen_items : DSList(N_ITEMS, DSBool())

# --- Constraints ---
def fit_item_in_box(item: Item, box: Box, x_position: DSInt(), y_position: DSInt()):
    assert x_position >= 0
    assert x_position + item.width <= box.width
    assert y_position >= 0
    assert y_position + item.height <= box.height

def assign_items_to_boxes(items: DSList(N_ITEMS, Item), box_assignment: DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment), boxes: DSList(N_ITEMS, Box)):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        box_assignment_item: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[i]
        box: Box = boxes[box_assignment_item.box_number]
        fit_item_in_box(item, box, box_assignment_item.x_position, box_assignment_item.y_position)

# --- Objective ---
def calculate_objective(items: DSList(N_ITEMS, Item), box_assignment: DSList(N_ITEMS, BoxAssignment)):
    objective: int = 0
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item: Item = items[i]
        box_assignment_item: BoxAssignment = box_assignment[i]
        objective = objective + item.width * item.height
    return objective

# --- Initialization ---

    {"width": ITEM1_WIDTH, "height": ITEM1_HEIGHT},
    {"width": ITEM2_WIDTH, "height": ITEM2_HEIGHT},

# --- Constraints ---

def check_no_overlap(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            item_i = item_box_assignment[i]
            item_j = item_box_assignment[j]
            if item_i.box_number == item_j.box_number:
                assert (item_i.x_position + item_i.width <= item_j.x_position) or \
                       (item_j.x_position + item_j.width <= item_i.x_position) or \
                       (item_i.y_position + item_i.height <= item_j.y_position) or \
                       (item_j.y_position + item_j.height <= item_i.y_position)

check_no_overlap(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)

def check_box_limits(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item = item_box_assignment[i]
        box = item_box_assignment[i].box_number
        x_position = x_y_positions[i].x_position
        y_position = x_y_positions[i].y_position
        item_width = item.width
        item_height = item.height
        assert x_position >= 0
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position >= 0
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

check_box_limits(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)

# --- Constraints ---

def check_no_overlap(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        for j in range(i + 1, N_ITEMS + 1):
            item_i = item_box_assignment[i]
            item_j = item_box_assignment[j]
            if item_i.box_number == item_j.box_number:
                assert (item_i.x_position + item_i.width <= item_j.x_position) or \
                       (item_j.x_position + item_j.width <= item_i.x_position) or \
                       (item_i.y_position + item_i.height <= item_j.y_position) or \
                       (item_j.y_position + item_j.height <= item_i.y_position)

check_no_overlap(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)

def check_box_limits(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item = item_box_assignment[i]
        box = item_box_assignment[i].box_number
        x_position = x_y_positions[i].x_position
        y_position = x_y_positions[i].y_position
        item_width = item.width
        item_height = item.height
        assert x_position >= 0
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position >= 0
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

check_box_limits(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)

def fit_item_in_box(item: Item, box_width: int, box_height: int):
    assert item.width <= box_width
    assert item.height <= box_height

def assign_positions(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionsArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_index = item_box_assignment[i].item_index
        box_index = item_box_assignment[i].box_index
        x_position = item_box_assignment[i].x_position
        y_position = item_box_assignment[i].y_position
        item_width = ITEM1_WIDTH if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_WIDTH if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_WIDTH if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_WIDTH if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_WIDTH if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_WIDTH
        item_height = ITEM1_HEIGHT if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_HEIGHT if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_HEIGHT if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_HEIGHT if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_HEIGHT if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_HEIGHT
        x_y_positions[i].x = x_position
        x_y_positions[i].y = y_position
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fit_item_in_box(ITEM1, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

        item_index = item_box_assignment[i].item_index

        x_position = item_box_assignment[i].x_position
        y_position = item_box_assignment[i].y_position
        item_width = ITEM1_WIDTH if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_WIDTH if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_WIDTH if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_WIDTH if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_WIDTH if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_WIDTH
        item_height = ITEM1_HEIGHT if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_HEIGHT if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_HEIGHT if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_HEIGHT if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_HEIGHT if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_HEIGHT
        x_y_positions[i].x = x_position
        x_y_positions[i].y = y_position
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

# --- Objects ---
Item = DSRecord({
    "width": DSInt(),
    "height": DSInt()
})

})

# --- Objects ---

# --- Constraints ---
def fit_item_in_box(item: Item, box_width: int, box_height: int):
    assert item.width <= box_width
    assert item.height <= box_height

def assign_positions(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionsArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_index = item_box_assignment[i].item_index
        box_index = item_box_assignment[i].box_index
        x_position = item_box_assignment[i].x_position
        y_position = item_box_assignment[i].y_position
        item_width = ITEM1_WIDTH if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_WIDTH if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_WIDTH if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_WIDTH if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_WIDTH if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_WIDTH
        item_height = ITEM1_HEIGHT if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_HEIGHT if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_HEIGHT if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_HEIGHT if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_HEIGHT if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_HEIGHT
        x_y_positions[i].x = x_position
        x_y_positions[i].y = y_position
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

fit_item_in_box(ITEM1, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM2, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM3, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM4, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM5, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM6, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

assign_positions(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)



# --- Objects ---

# --- Constraints ---
def fit_item_in_box(item: Item, box_width: int, box_height: int):
    assert item.width <= box_width
    assert item.height <= box_height

fit_item_in_box(ITEM1, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM2, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM3, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM4, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM5, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)
fit_item_in_box(ITEM6, BOX_WIDTH, BOX_HEIGHT)

def assign_positions(item_box_assignment: ItemBoxAssignmentArray, x_y_positions: XYPositionsArray):
    for i in range(1, N_ITEMS + 1):
        item_index = item_box_assignment[i].item_index
        box_index = item_box_assignment[i].box_index
        x_position = item_box_assignment[i].x_position
        y_position = item_box_assignment[i].y_position
        item_width = ITEM1_WIDTH if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_WIDTH if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_WIDTH if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_WIDTH if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_WIDTH if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_WIDTH
        item_height = ITEM1_HEIGHT if item_index == 1 else ITEM2_HEIGHT if item_index == 2 else ITEM3_HEIGHT if item_index == 3 else ITEM4_HEIGHT if item_index == 4 else ITEM5_HEIGHT if item_index == 5 else ITEM6_HEIGHT
        x_y_positions[i].x = x_position
        x_y_positions[i].y = y_position
        assert x_position + item_width <= BOX_WIDTH
        assert y_position + item_height <= BOX_HEIGHT

assign_positions(item_box_assignment, x_y_positions)

Process finished with exit code 0
